 The commission has sought information from the state's Chief Election Officer about the new delimitation
 ayog ab grih mantralay ke anurodh ke baad hi parisemen kii prakriya shuru karegaa

 Explain that along with Jammu and Kashmir being a union territory, an assembly will also be formed
 chunaav ayog ne is baithak main shuruaati charchaa kii
 Chief Election Commissioner Sunil Arora, both Election Commissioners and other senior officials of the Election Commission attended this meeting of the Election Commission
 gauratlab he ki jammu-kashmir ko centre shasit pradesh banaaya gaya he, saath hi ladakh ko alag kiya gaya he
 With Jammu and Kashmir being a union territory, there will also be an assembly, that is, there will be a state government, a cabinet
 vahiin ladakh sirf centre shasit pradesh hi rahegaa

 agar abhi kii baat karen to jammu-kashmir main kul 111 vidhansabha hai

 ayog kaa kahana he ki ye iviem ke suraksha maanakon ko majboot banane kii kavayad he naa ki iviem ko hack karne kaa muqabla

 lekin in mashiinon ke madraboard main badlaav yaa phir inhen apane saath le jane nahin diya jayega

 Mainpuri Lok Sabha seat background Mainpuri Lok Sabha seat has been in discussion since the first election held in the country
 1952 se lekar 1971 tak hue desh main kul 5 chunaav main yahaan se congress ne jeet darj kii thi
 Although the Congress was defeated by the Janata Party in the 1977 anti-incumbency wave, the Congress withdrew the seat in the by-elections held in 1978 the following year
 uske baad 1980 main congress se seat chhini par 1984 kii lahar main phir waapas ai
 The Congress won the last time here in 1984, after which this seat has been in the possession of regional parties
 1989 or 1991 main yahaan lagaataar janata party ne jeet darj kii
 But after forming the party in 1992, Mulayam Singh Yadav contested the 1996 election from here and also won by a large margin
 uske baad 1998, 1999 main bhi ye seat samaajawaadee party ke paas hi rahi
 Mulayam again returned to this seat in 2004, but later relinquished the seat
 2004 main dharmendra yadav yahaan se upachunaav main jite
 However, Mulayam returned here in the 2009 election and kept the seat with him
 2014 ke chunaav main bhi mulaayam ne yahaan se jeet darj kar apane pote tejpratap singh yadav ko ye seat de di

 ek channel se baat karte om puri ne bhartiya sainik ke liye kathith taur par apmanjanak tippanee main kaha tha ki un par kisi ne sena ne dabaav nahin daalaa tha
 MNS criticized Om Puri, calling him insensitive
 emenes ke film prakoshth ke adhyaksh amay khopakar ne kaha, abhi tak ham salmaan khan, mahesh bhatta or abu azmi ko hi betuke bayanon ke liye jaanate the lekin ab lagata he ki om puri ne unki jagah le lee he

 dilli hoicourt kii dabl bench ne swaraj india party kii yachika khaarij kar di he
 The party had demanded a common symbol in the MCD election
 hoicourt ne kaha- chunaav ayog is vakt niyamon main badlaav nahin kar saktaa
 Delhi Election Office cannot provide a common symbol without changing the rules
 hoicourt main pairvi ke liye swaraj india ke sasthaapak sadsy prashanth bhushan or unke pita shanti bhushan pahunche the
 The Delhi High Court had rejected the petition of Swaraj India on the issue of frustration met from the Singer Bench
 jiske baad swaraj india party ne dabl bench main apil kii thi
 But on Monday, the double bench also dismissed the petition, rejecting the party's demand
 darasal swaraj india ne court main chunaav ayog ke notification ko chunauti di thi
 The notification said that common symbols cannot be given to unregistered registered parties
 hoicourt kii single bench ne chunaav ayog ke notification ko sahi mana tha
 After the decision of the double bench, it has now been decided that the Swaraj India Party will have to contest the MCCD elections without a common symbol
 2013 main supreme court ne apane ek aadesh main kaha tha ki agar koi party 10 fisadi siton par chunaav ladati he to use kaaman simbel ek chunaav ladane ke liye diya ja saktaa he
 Based on this order, the common symbol of the broom was given to the Aam Aadmi Party in the assembly elections
 lekin emsidi chunaavon main dilli ellection offis ke prastaav par dilli sarkaar ne koi nirnay nahin liya
 Due to which Swaraj India could not get a common symbol
 bihar ke gaya main vishwa dharohar mahabodhi mandir kii chamak phir se lautne lagi he
 The work of cleaning the gold dome in the temple is going on
 gumbad kii plate kii safai ke liye khaastaur thailand se kaarigaron ko bulaayaa gaya he jo badi bareeki se plate kii safai kar rahe hai
 So that the gold sparkle can be returned once more
 mahabodhi mandir ke gumbad tak chadhane ke liye seedhi taiyaar kii gai he jis par chadhakar karigar isaki safai ke kaam main lage hai
 In 2013, Thailand's devotees made 289
 70 kilogram sone kii plate se gumbad ko lapeta tha jisase mandir kii chamak or bad gai thi
 In the last four years, there was dust on the gold dome, due to which the brightness of the dome faded
 jab thailand ke shraddhaluon kii najar gai to turant unhone isaki safai kaa nirnay liya
 For this reason, chemical washing has been started to brighten the dome of gold
 bodhgaya mandir management cameti ke sachiv nande daroje ne bataaya ki thailand ke shraddhaluon ne gumbad parsone kii plate lagaai thivhi thailand kaa group ab gumbad par lage sone kii plate kii safai main juta he, taaki uski chamak barkaraar rahe
